2026-05-19T21:11:02.3919600Z [36;1m  LIPO_OUT=$(lipo -info "$BIN" 2>&1)[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3919720Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3919870Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT" | grep -q "x86_64" || error "Missing x86_64 in $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3920090Z [36;1m  echo "$LIPO_OUT" | grep -q "arm64" || error "Missing arm64 in $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3920320Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3920450Z [36;1m  # Binary size check (should be > 1MB for a real plugin)[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3920670Z [36;1m  SIZE=$(stat -f%z "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || stat -c%s "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3920850Z [36;1m  if [ "$SIZE" -lt 1048576 ]; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3921190Z [36;1m    error "Binary suspiciously small ($SIZE bytes): $BIN"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3921370Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3921470Z [36;1m  echo "Binary size: $SIZE bytes"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3921580Z [36;1mdone[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3921660Z [36;1m[0m

2026-05-19T21:11:02.3922220Z [36;1m# 4. CODE SIGNATURE INTEGRITY[0m

2026-05-19T21:11:02.3922500Z [36;1mecho ""[0m

2026-05-19T21:11:02.3922820Z [36;1mecho "----------------------------"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3922950Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3923040Z [36;1mfor BUNDLE in "$VST3" "$CLAP"; do[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3923170Z [36;1m  echo "Checking $(basename $BUNDLE)..."[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3923300Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3923540Z [36;1m  # Strict signature verification (no --deep here, check bundle itself)[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3923820Z [36;1m  codesign -vvv "$BUNDLE" || error "Signature verification failed for $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3924110Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3924220Z [36;1m  # Verify signature is ad-hoc[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3924360Z [36;1m  CS_INFO=$(codesign -dvv "$BUNDLE" 2>&1)[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3924510Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3924700Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "Signature=adhoc" || error "Not ad-hoc signed: $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3925120Z [36;1m    # Allow either adhoc,runtime or just adhoc (macOS 15+ can't embed entitlements ad-hoc)[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3925360Z [36;1m    if echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "adhoc,runtime"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3925520Z [36;1m      echo "  Hardened runtime: enabled"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3925740Z [36;1m    else[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3925940Z [36;1m      echo "  Hardened runtime: disabled (expected — ad-hoc on macOS 15+ can't embed entitlements)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3926160Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3926320Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3926440Z [36;1m  # Verify CodeDirectory exists and is sealed[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3926680Z [36;1m  echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "Sealed Resources" || error "Sealed Resources missing: $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3927170Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3927300Z [36;1m  # Check that no files are modified after signing[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3927490Z [36;1m  if codesign -vvv "$BUNDLE" 2>&1 | grep -qi "modified"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3927690Z [36;1m    error "Files modified after signing in $(basename $BUNDLE)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3927930Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3928020Z [36;1mdone[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3928090Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3928170Z [36;1mecho "Code signature: OK"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3928280Z [36;1m[0m

2026-05-19T21:11:02.3928660Z [36;1m# 5. ENTITLEMENTS (skip if no hardened runtime — ad-hoc on macOS 15+ can't embed)[0m

2026-05-19T21:11:02.3929510Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3929590Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements() {[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3929700Z [36;1m  local BIN="$1"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3929790Z [36;1m  local NAME="$2"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3929940Z [36;1m  local CS_INFO=$(codesign -dvv "$BIN" 2>&1 || echo "")[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3930110Z [36;1m  if echo "$CS_INFO" | grep -q "runtime"; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3930370Z [36;1m    # Hardened runtime is enabled — check entitlements[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3930610Z [36;1m    local ENTITLEMENTS=$(codesign -d --entitlements - "$BIN" 2>/dev/null || echo "")[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3930820Z [36;1m    if [ -z "$ENTITLEMENTS" ]; then[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3931060Z [36;1m      error "No entitlements found in $NAME (has hardened runtime)"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3931250Z [36;1m    else[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3931440Z [36;1m      echo "$ENTITLEMENTS" | grep -q "com.apple.security.cs.disable-library-validation" || \[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3931810Z [36;1m        error "Missing disable-library-validation entitlement in $NAME"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932000Z [36;1m    fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932090Z [36;1m  else[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932230Z [36;1m    echo "SKIP: $NAME has no hardened runtime — entitlements not applicable"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932430Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932590Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932700Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932790Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements "$VST3_BIN" "VST3"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3932930Z [36;1mcheck_entitlements "$CLAP_BIN" "CLAP"[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3933060Z [36;1m[0m
2026-05-19T21:11:02.3933160Z [36;1mecho "Entitlements: OK"[0m
